                  ? CFG_GLPI['root_doc']+'/public/lib/tinymce/skins/ui/oxide-dark'
                  : CFG_GLPI['root_doc']+'/public/lib/tinymce/skins/ui/oxide',
               body_class: 'rich_text_container',
               content_css: '/glpi/css_compiled/css_palettes_auror.min.css,/glpi/public/lib/base.min.css',

               min_height: 150,
               resize: true,

               // disable path indicator in bottom bar
               elementpath: false,

               // inline toolbar configuration
               menubar: false,
               toolbar: richtext_layout == 'classic'
                  ? 'styles | bold italic | forecolor backcolor | bullist numlist outdent indent | emoticons table link image | code fullscreen'
                  : false,
               quickbars_insert_toolbar: richtext_layout == 'inline'
                  ? 'emoticons quicktable quickimage quicklink | bullist numlist | outdent indent '
                  : false,
               quickbars_selection_toolbar: richtext_layout == 'inline'
                  ? 'bold italic | styles | forecolor backcolor '
                  : false,
               contextmenu: richtext_layout == 'classic'
                  ? false
                  : 'copy paste | emoticons table image link | undo redo | code fullscreen',

               // Content settings
               entity_encoding: 'raw',
               invalid_elements: 'applet,canvas,embed,form,object,iframe',
               readonly: false,
               relative_urls: false,
               remove_script_host: false,

               browser_spellcheck: true,
               cache_suffix: '?v=4606a55b6893b74e722e1cf6668f5db6cf2890e3',

               setup: function(editor) {
                  // "required" state handling
                  if ($('#content_252985843').attr('required') == 'required') {
                     $('#content_252985843').removeAttr('required'); // Necessary to bypass browser validation

                     editor.on('submit', function (e) {
                        if ($('#content_252985843').val() == '') {
                           const field = $('#content_252985843').closest('.form-field').find('label').text().replace('*', '').trim();
                           alert(__('The %s field is mandatory').replace('%s', field));
                           e.preventDefault();

                           // Prevent other events to run
                           // Needed to not break single submit forms
                           e.stopPropagation();
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('keyup', function (e) {
                        editor.save();
                        if ($('#content_252985843').val() == '') {
                           $(editor.container).addClass('required');
                        } else {
                           $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('init', function (e) {
                        if (strip_tags($('#content_252985843').val()) == '') {
                           $(editor.container).addClass('required');
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('paste', function (e) {
                        // Remove required on paste event
                        // This is only needed when pasting with right click (context menu)
                        // Pasting with Ctrl+V is already handled by keyup event above
                        $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                     });
                  }

                  editor.on('Change', function (e) {
                     // Nothing fancy here. Since this is only used for tracking unsaved changes,
                     // we want to keep the logic in common.js with the other form input events.
                     onTinyMCEChange(e);
                  });
                  // ctrl + enter submit the parent form
                  editor.addShortcut('ctrl+13', 'submit', function() {
                     editor.save();
                     submitparentForm($('#content_252985843'));
                  });
               }
            }, {"language":"pt_BR","language_url":"\/glpi\/public\/lib\/tinymce-i18n\/langs6\/pt_BR.js"}));
         });

               dataType: 'json',
               type: 'POST',
               data: function (params) {
                  query = params;
                  return $.extend({}, params_dropdown_itilfollowuptemplates_id252985843, {
                     searchText: params.term,
                     page_limit: 10, // page size

               processResults: function (data, params) {

                  _one_id: value,
               }),
               dataType: 'json',
               type: 'POST',
            }).done(function(data) {

               var iterate_options = function(options, value) {
                  var to_return = false;
                  $.each(options, function(index, option) {
                     if (option.hasOwnProperty('id')
                         && option.id == value) {
                        to_return = option;
                        return false; // act as break;
                     }

                     if (option.hasOwnProperty('children')) {
                        to_return = iterate_options(option.children, value);
                     }
                  });

                  return to_return;
               };

               var option = iterate_options(data.results, value);
               if (option !== false) {
                  var newOption = new Option(option.text, option.id, true, true);
                   $('#dropdown_itilfollowuptemplates_id252985843').append(newOption).trigger('change');
               }
            });
         });

      <script type="text/javascript">
         function itilfollowuptemplate_update252985843(value) {
            $.ajax({
               url: '/glpi/ajax/itilfollowup.php',
               type: 'POST',
               data: {
                  itilfollowuptemplates_id: value,
                  items_id: '57099',
                  itemtype: 'Ticket'
               }
            }).done(function (data) {
               var requesttypes_id = isNaN(parseInt(data.requesttypes_id))
                  ? 0
                  : parseInt(data.requesttypes_id);

               // set textarea content
               if (tasktinymce = tinymce.get("content_252985843")) {
                  tasktinymce.setContent(data.content);
               }
               // set category
               //need to create new DOM option, because SELECT is remotely-sourced (AJAX)
               //see : https://select2.org/programmatic-control/add-select-clear-items#preselecting-options-in-an-remotely-sourced-ajax-select2
               var newOption = new Option(data.requesttypes_name, requesttypes_id, true, true);
               $("#dropdown_requesttypes_id252985843").append(newOption).trigger('change');

               // set is_private
               $("#is_private_252985843")
                  .prop("checked", data.is_private == "0"
                     ? false
                     : true);
            });
         }
      </script>

                  </div>
               </div>
            </div>

               setup: function(editor) {
                  // "required" state handling
                  if ($('#content_399489805').attr('required') == 'required') {
                     $('#content_399489805').removeAttr('required'); // Necessary to bypass browser validation

                     editor.on('submit', function (e) {
                        if ($('#content_399489805').val() == '') {
                           const field = $('#content_399489805').closest('.form-field').find('label').text().replace('*', '').trim();
                           alert(__('The %s field is mandatory').replace('%s', field));
                           e.preventDefault();

                           // Prevent other events to run
                           // Needed to not break single submit forms
                           e.stopPropagation();
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('keyup', function (e) {
                        editor.save();
                        if ($('#content_399489805').val() == '') {
                           $(editor.container).addClass('required');
                        } else {
                           $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('init', function (e) {
                        if (strip_tags($('#content_399489805').val()) == '') {
                           $(editor.container).addClass('required');
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('paste', function (e) {
                        // Remove required on paste event
                        // This is only needed when pasting with right click (context menu)
                        // Pasting with Ctrl+V is already handled by keyup event above
                        $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                     });
                  }

                  editor.on('Change', function (e) {
                     // Nothing fancy here. Since this is only used for tracking unsaved changes,
                     // we want to keep the logic in common.js with the other form input events.
                     onTinyMCEChange(e);
                  });
                  // ctrl + enter submit the parent form
                  editor.addShortcut('ctrl+13', 'submit', function() {
                     editor.save();
                     submitparentForm($('#content_399489805'));
                  });
               }
            }, {"language":"pt_BR","language_url":"\/glpi\/public\/lib\/tinymce-i18n\/langs6\/pt_BR.js"}));
         });

//<![CDATA[

$(function() {
         const select2_el = $('#dropdown_state399489805').select2({
            
            width: '100%',
            dropdownAutoWidth: true,
            dropdownParent: $('#dropdown_state399489805').closest('div.modal, div.dropdown-menu, body'),
            quietMillis: 100,
            minimumResultsForSearch: 5,
            matcher: function(params, data) {
               // store last search in the global var
               query = params;

               // If there are no search terms, return all of the data
               if ($.trim(params.term) === '') {
                  return data;
               }

               var searched_term = getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(params.term);
               var data_text = typeof(data.text) === 'string'
                  ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(data.text)
                  : '';
               var select2_fuzzy_opts = {
                  pre: '<span class="select2-rendered__match">',
                  post: '</span>',
               };

               if (data_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || data_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                  // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                  data_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(data_text);
               }

               // Skip if there is no 'children' property
               if (typeof data.children === 'undefined') {
                  var match  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match == null) {
                     return false;
                  }
                  data.rendered_text = match.rendered_text;
                  data.score = match.score;
                  return data;
               }

               // `data.children` contains the actual options that we are matching against
               // also check in `data.text` (optgroup title)
               var filteredChildren = [];

               $.each(data.children, function (idx, child) {
                  var child_text = typeof(child.text) === 'string'
                     ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(child.text)
                     : '';

                  if (child_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || child_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                     // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                     child_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(child_text);
                  }

                  var match_child = fuzzy.match(searched_term, child_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  var match_text  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match_child !== null || match_text !== null) {
                     if (match_text !== null) {
                        data.score         = match_text.score;
                        data.rendered_text = match_text.rendered;
                     }

                     if (match_child !== null) {
                        child.score         = match_child.score;
                        child.rendered_text = match_child.rendered;
                     }
                     filteredChildren.push(child);
                  }
               });

               // If we matched any of the group's children, then set the matched children on the group
               // and return the group object
               if (filteredChildren.length) {
                  var modifiedData = $.extend({}, data, true);
                  modifiedData.children = filteredChildren;

                  // You can return modified objects from here
                  // This includes matching the `children` how you want in nested data sets
                  return modifiedData;
               }

               // Return `null` if the term should not be displayed
               return null;
            },
            templateResult: templateResult,
            templateSelection: templateSelection,
         })
         .bind('setValue', function(e, value) {
            $('#dropdown_state399489805').val(value).trigger('change');
         })
         $('label[for=dropdown_state399489805]').on('click', function(){ $('#dropdown_state399489805').select2('open'); });
         $('#dropdown_state399489805').on('select2:open', function(e){
            const search_input = document.querySelector(`.select2-search__field[aria-controls='select2-${e.target.id}-results']`);
            if (search_input) {
               search_input.focus();
            }
         });
      });

//]]>
</script>   
         
      </div>
   </div>

//<![CDATA[

$(function() {
         const select2_el = $('#dropdown_actiontime399489805').select2({
            
            width: '100%',
            dropdownAutoWidth: true,
            dropdownParent: $('#dropdown_actiontime399489805').closest('div.modal, div.dropdown-menu, body'),
            quietMillis: 100,
            minimumResultsForSearch: 5,
            matcher: function(params, data) {
               // store last search in the global var
               query = params;

               // If there are no search terms, return all of the data
               if ($.trim(params.term) === '') {
                  return data;
               }

               var searched_term = getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(params.term);
               var data_text = typeof(data.text) === 'string'
                  ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(data.text)
                  : '';
               var select2_fuzzy_opts = {
                  pre: '<span class="select2-rendered__match">',
                  post: '</span>',
               };

               if (data_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || data_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                  // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                  data_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(data_text);
               }

               // Skip if there is no 'children' property
               if (typeof data.children === 'undefined') {
                  var match  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match == null) {
                     return false;
                  }
                  data.rendered_text = match.rendered_text;
                  data.score = match.score;
                  return data;
               }

               // `data.children` contains the actual options that we are matching against
               // also check in `data.text` (optgroup title)
               var filteredChildren = [];

               $.each(data.children, function (idx, child) {
                  var child_text = typeof(child.text) === 'string'
                     ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(child.text)
                     : '';

                  if (child_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || child_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                     // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                     child_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(child_text);
                  }

                  var match_child = fuzzy.match(searched_term, child_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  var match_text  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match_child !== null || match_text !== null) {
                     if (match_text !== null) {
                        data.score         = match_text.score;
                        data.rendered_text = match_text.rendered;
                     }

                     if (match_child !== null) {
                        child.score         = match_child.score;
                        child.rendered_text = match_child.rendered;
                     }
                     filteredChildren.push(child);
                  }
               });

               // If we matched any of the group's children, then set the matched children on the group
               // and return the group object
               if (filteredChildren.length) {
                  var modifiedData = $.extend({}, data, true);
                  modifiedData.children = filteredChildren;

                  // You can return modified objects from here
                  // This includes matching the `children` how you want in nested data sets
                  return modifiedData;
               }

               // Return `null` if the term should not be displayed
               return null;
            },
            templateResult: templateResult,
            templateSelection: templateSelection,
         })
         .bind('setValue', function(e, value) {
            $('#dropdown_actiontime399489805').val(value).trigger('change');
         })
         $('label[for=dropdown_actiontime399489805]').on('click', function(){ $('#dropdown_actiontime399489805').select2('open'); });
         $('#dropdown_actiontime399489805').on('select2:open', function(e){
            const search_input = document.querySelector(`.select2-search__field[aria-controls='select2-${e.target.id}-results']`);
            if (search_input) {
               search_input.focus();
            }
         });
      });

//]]>
</script>   
         
      </div>
   </div>

         <select name="followup_frequency" id="dropdown_followup_frequency399489805" class="form-select select2-hidden-accessible" size="1" data-select2-id="dropdown_followup_frequency399489805" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true"><option value="0" data-select2-id="21">Desabilitado</option><option value="86400">Todos os dias</option><option value="172800">A cada dois dias</option><option value="259200">A cada três dias</option><option value="345600">A cada quatro dias</option><option value="432000">A cada cinco dias</option><option value="518400">A cada seis dias</option><option value="604800">A cada semana</option><option value="1209600">A cada duas semanas</option><option value="1814400">A cada três semanas</option><option value="2419200">A cada quatro semanas</option></select><span class="select2 select2-container select2-container--default" dir="ltr" data-select2-id="20" style="width: 95%;"><span class="selection"><span class="select2-selection select2-selection--single" role="combobox" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0" aria-disabled="false" aria-labelledby="select2-dropdown_followup_frequency399489805-container"><span class="select2-selection__rendered" id="select2-dropdown_followup_frequency399489805-container" role="textbox" aria-readonly="true" title="Desabilitado"><span>Desabilitado</span></span><span class="select2-selection__arrow" role="presentation"><b role="presentation"></b></span></span></span><span class="dropdown-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"></span></span><script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

$(function() {
         const select2_el = $('#dropdown_followup_frequency399489805').select2({
            
            width: '95%',
            dropdownAutoWidth: true,
            dropdownParent: $('#dropdown_followup_frequency399489805').closest('div.modal, div.dropdown-menu, body'),
            quietMillis: 100,
            minimumResultsForSearch: 5,
            matcher: function(params, data) {
               // store last search in the global var
               query = params;

               // If there are no search terms, return all of the data
               if ($.trim(params.term) === '') {
                  return data;
               }

               var searched_term = getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(params.term);
               var data_text = typeof(data.text) === 'string'
                  ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(data.text)
                  : '';
               var select2_fuzzy_opts = {
                  pre: '<span class="select2-rendered__match">',
                  post: '</span>',
               };

               if (data_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || data_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                  // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                  data_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(data_text);
               }

               // Skip if there is no 'children' property
               if (typeof data.children === 'undefined') {
                  var match  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match == null) {
                     return false;
                  }
                  data.rendered_text = match.rendered_text;
                  data.score = match.score;
                  return data;
               }

               // `data.children` contains the actual options that we are matching against
               // also check in `data.text` (optgroup title)
               var filteredChildren = [];

               $.each(data.children, function (idx, child) {
                  var child_text = typeof(child.text) === 'string'
                     ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(child.text)
                     : '';

                  if (child_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || child_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                     // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                     child_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(child_text);
                  }

                  var match_child = fuzzy.match(searched_term, child_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  var match_text  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match_child !== null || match_text !== null) {
                     if (match_text !== null) {
                        data.score         = match_text.score;
                        data.rendered_text = match_text.rendered;
                     }

                     if (match_child !== null) {
                        child.score         = match_child.score;
                        child.rendered_text = match_child.rendered;
                     }
                     filteredChildren.push(child);
                  }
               });

               // If we matched any of the group's children, then set the matched children on the group
               // and return the group object
               if (filteredChildren.length) {
                  var modifiedData = $.extend({}, data, true);
                  modifiedData.children = filteredChildren;

                  // You can return modified objects from here
                  // This includes matching the `children` how you want in nested data sets
                  return modifiedData;
               }

               // Return `null` if the term should not be displayed
               return null;
            },
            templateResult: templateResult,
            templateSelection: templateSelection,
         })
         .bind('setValue', function(e, value) {
            $('#dropdown_followup_frequency399489805').val(value).trigger('change');
         })
         $('label[for=dropdown_followup_frequency399489805]').on('click', function(){ $('#dropdown_followup_frequency399489805').select2('open'); });
         $('#dropdown_followup_frequency399489805').on('select2:open', function(e){
            const search_input = document.querySelector(`.select2-search__field[aria-controls='select2-${e.target.id}-results']`);
            if (search_input) {
               search_input.focus();
            }
         });
      });

//]]>
</script>
         
      </div>
   </div>

      <script type="text/javascript">
         function itiltasktemplate_update399489805(value) {
            $.ajax({
               url: '/glpi/ajax/task.php',
               type: 'POST',
               data: {
                  tasktemplates_id: value,
                  items_id: '57099',
                  itemtype: 'Ticket'
               }
            }).done(function (data) {
                if (data.content !== undefined) {
                    // set textarea content
                    if (tasktinymce = tinymce.get("content_399489805")) {
                        tasktinymce.setContent(data.content);
                    }
                }

                if (data.taskcategories_id !== undefined) {
                    // set category
                    const taskcategories_id = isNaN(parseInt(data.taskcategories_id))
                        ? 0
                        : parseInt(data.taskcategories_id);

                     //need to create new DOM option, because SELECT is remotely-sourced (AJAX)
                     //see : https://select2.org/programmatic-control/add-select-clear-items#preselecting-options-in-an-remotely-sourced-ajax-select2
                     var newOption = new Option(data.taskcategories_name, taskcategories_id, true, true);
                     $("#dropdown_taskcategories_id399489805").append(newOption).trigger('change');
                }

                if (data.is_private !== undefined) {
                    // set is_private
                    $("#is_private_399489805")
                        .prop("checked", data.is_private == "0"
                            ? false
                            : true);
                }

                if (data.state !== undefined) {
                    // Set state
                    $("#dropdown_state399489805").trigger('setValue', data.state);
                }

                if (data.actiontime !== undefined) {
                    // Set duration
                    $("#dropdown_actiontime399489805").trigger('setValue', data.actiontime);
                }

                if (data.users_id_tech !== undefined) {
                    // Set user
                    $("#dropdown_users_id_tech399489805").trigger('setValue', data.users_id_tech);
                }

               if (data.groups_id_tech !== undefined) {
                   // Set group
                   $("#dropdown_groups_id_tech399489805").trigger('setValue', data.groups_id_tech);
               }
            });
         }
      </script>

                  if ($('#content_790314203').attr('required') == 'required') {
                     $('#content_790314203').removeAttr('required'); // Necessary to bypass browser validation

                     editor.on('submit', function (e) {
                        if ($('#content_790314203').val() == '') {
                           const field = $('#content_790314203').closest('.form-field').find('label').text().replace('*', '').trim();
                           alert(__('The %s field is mandatory').replace('%s', field));

                           e.stopPropagation();

                        editor.save();

                        } else {
                           $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                        }

                        // Remove required on paste event
                        // This is only needed when pasting with right click (context menu)
                        // Pasting with Ctrl+V is already handled by keyup event above
                        $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                     });
                  }

                  editor.on('Change', function (e) {
                     // Nothing fancy here. Since this is only used for tracking unsaved changes,
                     // we want to keep the logic in common.js with the other form input events.
                     onTinyMCEChange(e);
                  });
                  // ctrl + enter submit the parent form
                  editor.addShortcut('ctrl+13', 'submit', function() {
                     editor.save();
                     submitparentForm($('#content_790314203'));
                  });
               }

               }),
               dataType: 'json',
               type: 'POST',
            }).done(function(data) {

               var iterate_options = function(options, value) {
                  var to_return = false;
                  $.each(options, function(index, option) {
                     if (option.hasOwnProperty('id')
                         && option.id == value) {
                        to_return = option;
                        return false; // act as break;

                     if (option.hasOwnProperty('children')) {
                        to_return = iterate_options(option.children, value);
                     }
                  });

               };

               if (option !== false) {
                  var newOption = new Option(option.text, option.id, true, true);
                   $('#dropdown_solutiontypes_id790314203').append(newOption).trigger('change');
               }

               <select name="validatortype" id="dropdown_validatortype822323297" class="form-select select2-hidden-accessible" size="1" data-select2-id="dropdown_validatortype822323297" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true"><option value="0" data-select2-id="28">-----</option><option value="User">Usuário</option><option value="Group">Grupo</option></select><span class="select2 select2-container select2-container--default" dir="ltr" data-select2-id="27" style="width: 100%;"><span class="selection"><span class="select2-selection select2-selection--single" role="combobox" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0" aria-disabled="false" aria-labelledby="select2-dropdown_validatortype822323297-container"><span class="select2-selection__rendered" id="select2-dropdown_validatortype822323297-container" role="textbox" aria-readonly="true" title="-----"><span>-----</span></span><span class="select2-selection__arrow" role="presentation"><b role="presentation"></b></span></span></span><span class="dropdown-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"></span></span><script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

$(function() {
         const select2_el = $('#dropdown_validatortype822323297').select2({
            
            width: '100%',
            dropdownAutoWidth: true,
            dropdownParent: $('#dropdown_validatortype822323297').closest('div.modal, div.dropdown-menu, body'),
            quietMillis: 100,
            minimumResultsForSearch: 5,
            matcher: function(params, data) {
               // store last search in the global var
               query = params;

               // If there are no search terms, return all of the data
               if ($.trim(params.term) === '') {
                  return data;
               }

               var searched_term = getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(params.term);
               var data_text = typeof(data.text) === 'string'
                  ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(data.text)
                  : '';
               var select2_fuzzy_opts = {
                  pre: '<span class="select2-rendered__match">',
                  post: '</span>',
               };

               if (data_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || data_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                  // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                  data_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(data_text);
               }

               // Skip if there is no 'children' property
               if (typeof data.children === 'undefined') {
                  var match  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match == null) {
                     return false;
                  }
                  data.rendered_text = match.rendered_text;
                  data.score = match.score;
                  return data;
               }

               // `data.children` contains the actual options that we are matching against
               // also check in `data.text` (optgroup title)
               var filteredChildren = [];

               $.each(data.children, function (idx, child) {
                  var child_text = typeof(child.text) === 'string'
                     ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(child.text)
                     : '';

                  if (child_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || child_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                     // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                     child_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(child_text);
                  }

                  var match_child = fuzzy.match(searched_term, child_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  var match_text  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match_child !== null || match_text !== null) {
                     if (match_text !== null) {
                        data.score         = match_text.score;
                        data.rendered_text = match_text.rendered;
                     }

                     if (match_child !== null) {
                        child.score         = match_child.score;
                        child.rendered_text = match_child.rendered;
                     }
                     filteredChildren.push(child);
                  }
               });

               // If we matched any of the group's children, then set the matched children on the group
               // and return the group object
               if (filteredChildren.length) {
                  var modifiedData = $.extend({}, data, true);
                  modifiedData.children = filteredChildren;

                  // You can return modified objects from here
                  // This includes matching the `children` how you want in nested data sets
                  return modifiedData;
               }

               // Return `null` if the term should not be displayed
               return null;
            },
            templateResult: templateResult,
            templateSelection: templateSelection,
         })
         .bind('setValue', function(e, value) {
            $('#dropdown_validatortype822323297').val(value).trigger('change');
         })
         $('label[for=dropdown_validatortype822323297]').on('click', function(){ $('#dropdown_validatortype822323297').select2('open'); });
         $('#dropdown_validatortype822323297').on('select2:open', function(e){
            const search_input = document.querySelector(`.select2-search__field[aria-controls='select2-${e.target.id}-results']`);
            if (search_input) {
               search_input.focus();
            }
         });
      });

//]]>
</script>   
         <span id="show_validator_field822323297" class="flex-grow-1">&nbsp;</span>
      </div>
   </div>

         <script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

         $(function() {
            var is_dark = $('html').css('--is-dark').trim() === 'true';
            var richtext_layout = "classic";

            // init editor
            tinyMCE.init(Object.assign({
               link_default_target: '_blank',
               branding: false,
               selector: '#comment_submission_822323297',
               text_patterns: false,

               plugins: ["autoresize","code","directionality","fullscreen","link","lists","quickbars","searchreplace","table","image","glpi_upload_doc","emoticons"],

               // Appearance
               skin_url: is_dark
                  ? CFG_GLPI['root_doc']+'/public/lib/tinymce/skins/ui/oxide-dark'
                  : CFG_GLPI['root_doc']+'/public/lib/tinymce/skins/ui/oxide',
               body_class: 'rich_text_container',
               content_css: '/glpi/css_compiled/css_palettes_auror.min.css,/glpi/public/lib/base.min.css',

               min_height: 150,
               resize: true,

               // disable path indicator in bottom bar
               elementpath: false,

               // inline toolbar configuration
               menubar: false,
               toolbar: richtext_layout == 'classic'
                  ? 'styles | bold italic | forecolor backcolor | bullist numlist outdent indent | emoticons table link image | code fullscreen'
                  : false,
               quickbars_insert_toolbar: richtext_layout == 'inline'
                  ? 'emoticons quicktable quickimage quicklink | bullist numlist | outdent indent '
                  : false,
               quickbars_selection_toolbar: richtext_layout == 'inline'
                  ? 'bold italic | styles | forecolor backcolor '
                  : false,
               contextmenu: richtext_layout == 'classic'
                  ? false
                  : 'copy paste | emoticons table image link | undo redo | code fullscreen',

               // Content settings
               entity_encoding: 'raw',
               invalid_elements: 'applet,canvas,embed,form,object,iframe',
               readonly: false,
               relative_urls: false,
               remove_script_host: false,

               // Misc options
               browser_spellcheck: true,
               cache_suffix: '?v=4606a55b6893b74e722e1cf6668f5db6cf2890e3',

               setup: function(editor) {
                  // "required" state handling
                  if ($('#comment_submission_822323297').attr('required') == 'required') {
                     $('#comment_submission_822323297').removeAttr('required'); // Necessary to bypass browser validation

                     editor.on('submit', function (e) {
                        if ($('#comment_submission_822323297').val() == '') {
                           const field = $('#comment_submission_822323297').closest('.form-field').find('label').text().replace('*', '').trim();
                           alert(__('The %s field is mandatory').replace('%s', field));
                           e.preventDefault();

                           // Prevent other events to run
                           // Needed to not break single submit forms
                           e.stopPropagation();
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('keyup', function (e) {
                        editor.save();
                        if ($('#comment_submission_822323297').val() == '') {
                           $(editor.container).addClass('required');
                        } else {
                           $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('init', function (e) {
                        if (strip_tags($('#comment_submission_822323297').val()) == '') {
                           $(editor.container).addClass('required');
                        }
                     });
                     editor.on('paste', function (e) {
                        // Remove required on paste event
                        // This is only needed when pasting with right click (context menu)
                        // Pasting with Ctrl+V is already handled by keyup event above
                        $(editor.container).removeClass('required');
                     });
                  }

                  editor.on('Change', function (e) {
                     // Nothing fancy here. Since this is only used for tracking unsaved changes,
                     // we want to keep the logic in common.js with the other form input events.
                     onTinyMCEChange(e);
                  });
                  // ctrl + enter submit the parent form
                  editor.addShortcut('ctrl+13', 'submit', function() {
                     editor.save();
                     submitparentForm($('#comment_submission_822323297'));
                  });
               }
            }, {"language":"pt_BR","language_url":"\/glpi\/public\/lib\/tinymce-i18n\/langs6\/pt_BR.js"}));
         });

//]]>
</script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
         function change_task_state(tasks_id, target) {
            $.post('/glpi/ajax/timeline.php',
               {'action':     'change_task_state',
                  'tasks_id':   tasks_id,
                  'parenttype': 'Ticket',
                  'tickets_id': 57099
               })
               .done(function(response) {
                  $(target).closest('.timeline-item').find('.state')
                     .removeClass('state_1 state_2')
                     .addClass('state_'+response.state)
                     .attr('title', response.label);

                  $(target).closest('.timeline-item').find('.read-only-content')
                     .toggleClass('done');

                  var todo_tasks   = $('.todo-list-state .state.state_1').length;
                  var done_tasks   = $('.todo-list-state .state.state_2').length;
                  var total_tasks  = todo_tasks + done_tasks;
                  var percent_done = Math.floor(100 * done_tasks / total_tasks);

                  $('.timeline-progress')
                     .css('width', percent_done + '%')
                     .attr('aria-valuenow', percent_done);
                  $('.task-progress-label').html(percent_done + '%');
               });
         }
      </script>

$(function() {
   $(document).on("click", ".edit-timeline-item", function() {

      var content_block = timeline_item.find(".timeline-content");

         .find(".ajax-content")
         .html('<i class="fas fa-3x fa-spinner fa-spin ms-auto"></i>')
         .load("/glpi/ajax/timeline.php", {

            'type'       : itemtype,
            'parenttype' : 'Ticket',
            'tickets_id': 57099,
            'id'         : items_id,
            'item_action': item_action
         });

      timeline_item.find('.timeline-item-buttons').addClass('d-none');
      timeline_item.find('.close-edit-content').removeClass('d-none');

      $("#itil-footer").find(".main-actions").hide();
   });

   $(document).on("click", ".close-edit-content", function() {
      var timeline_item = $(this).closest(".timeline-item");
      timeline_item.find('.timeline-item-buttons').removeClass('d-none');
      timeline_item.find('.close-edit-content').addClass('d-none');

      timeline_item.find('.ajax-content').html('');
      timeline_item.find('.read-only-content').show();

      $("#itil-footer .main-actions").show();
   });
});

//<![CDATA[

$(function() {
         const select2_el = $('#dropdown_type130719115').select2({
            
            width: '100%',
            dropdownAutoWidth: true,
            dropdownParent: $('#dropdown_type130719115').closest('div.modal, div.dropdown-menu, body'),
            quietMillis: 100,
            minimumResultsForSearch: 5,
            matcher: function(params, data) {
               // store last search in the global var
               query = params;

               // If there are no search terms, return all of the data
               if ($.trim(params.term) === '') {
                  return data;
               }

               var searched_term = getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(params.term);
               var data_text = typeof(data.text) === 'string'
                  ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(data.text)
                  : '';
               var select2_fuzzy_opts = {
                  pre: '<span class="select2-rendered__match">',
                  post: '</span>',
               };

               if (data_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || data_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                  // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                  data_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(data_text);
               }

               // Skip if there is no 'children' property
               if (typeof data.children === 'undefined') {
                  var match  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match == null) {
                     return false;
                  }
                  data.rendered_text = match.rendered_text;
                  data.score = match.score;
                  return data;
               }

               // `data.children` contains the actual options that we are matching against
               // also check in `data.text` (optgroup title)
               var filteredChildren = [];

               $.each(data.children, function (idx, child) {
                  var child_text = typeof(child.text) === 'string'
                     ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(child.text)
                     : '';

                  if (child_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || child_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                     // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                     child_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(child_text);
                  }

                  var match_child = fuzzy.match(searched_term, child_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  var match_text  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match_child !== null || match_text !== null) {
                     if (match_text !== null) {
                        data.score         = match_text.score;
                        data.rendered_text = match_text.rendered;
                     }

                     if (match_child !== null) {
                        child.score         = match_child.score;
                        child.rendered_text = match_child.rendered;
                     }
                     filteredChildren.push(child);
                  }
               });

               // If we matched any of the group's children, then set the matched children on the group
               // and return the group object
               if (filteredChildren.length) {
                  var modifiedData = $.extend({}, data, true);
                  modifiedData.children = filteredChildren;

                  // You can return modified objects from here
                  // This includes matching the `children` how you want in nested data sets
                  return modifiedData;
               }

               // Return `null` if the term should not be displayed
               return null;
            },
            templateResult: templateResult,
            templateSelection: templateSelection,
         })
         .bind('setValue', function(e, value) {
            $('#dropdown_type130719115').val(value).trigger('change');
         })
         $('label[for=dropdown_type130719115]').on('click', function(){ $('#dropdown_type130719115').select2('open'); });
         $('#dropdown_type130719115').on('select2:open', function(e){
            const search_input = document.querySelector(`.select2-search__field[aria-controls='select2-${e.target.id}-results']`);
            if (search_input) {
               search_input.focus();
            }
         });
      });

//]]>
</script>

               };

               if (data_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || data_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                  // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                  data_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(data_text);
               }

               // Skip if there is no 'children' property
               if (typeof data.children === 'undefined') {
                  var match  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match == null) {
                     return false;
                  }
                  data.rendered_text = match.rendered_text;
                  data.score = match.score;
                  return data;
               }

               // `data.children` contains the actual options that we are matching against
               // also check in `data.text` (optgroup title)
               var filteredChildren = [];

               $.each(data.children, function (idx, child) {
                  var child_text = typeof(child.text) === 'string'
                     ? getTextWithoutDiacriticalMarks(child.text)
                     : '';

                  if (child_text.indexOf('>') !== -1 || child_text.indexOf('<') !== -1) {
                     // escape text, if it contains chevrons (can already be escaped prior to this point :/)
                     child_text = jQuery.fn.select2.defaults.defaults.escapeMarkup(child_text);
                  }

                  var match_child = fuzzy.match(searched_term, child_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  var match_text  = fuzzy.match(searched_term, data_text, select2_fuzzy_opts);
                  if (match_child !== null || match_text !== null) {
                     if (match_text !== null) {
                        data.score         = match_text.score;
                        data.rendered_text = match_text.rendered;
                     }

                     if (match_child !== null) {
                        child.score         = match_child.score;
                        child.rendered_text = match_child.rendered;
                     }
                     filteredChildren.push(child);
                  }
               });

               // If we matched any of the group's children, then set the matched children on the group
               // and return the group object
               if (filteredChildren.length) {
                  var modifiedData = $.extend({}, data, true);
                  modifiedData.children = filteredChildren;

                  // You can return modified objects from here
                  // This includes matching the `children` how you want in nested data sets
                  return modifiedData;
               }

               // Return `null` if the term should not be displayed
               return null;
            },
            templateResult: templateItilPriority,
            templateSelection: templateItilPriority,
         })
         .bind('setValue', function(e, value) {
            $('#dropdown_priority220110994').val(value).trigger('change');
         })
         $('label[for=dropdown_priority220110994]').on('click', function(){ $('#dropdown_priority220110994').select2('open'); });
         $('#dropdown_priority220110994').on('select2:open', function(e){
            const search_input = document.querySelector(`.select2-search__field[aria-controls='select2-${e.target.id}-results']`);
            if (search_input) {
               search_input.focus();
            }
         });
      });

//]]>
</script>
         
      </div>
   </div>

   $(function() {
      var actorytype = 'requester';

      // function to display an option in the list or the selected input
      var genericTemplate_147568279 = function(option = {}, is_selection = false) {
         var element   = $(option.element);
         var itemtype  = element.data('itemtype') ?? option.itemtype;
         var items_id  = element.data('items-id') ?? option.items_id;
         var text      = escapeMarkupText(element.data('text') ?? option.text ?? '');
         var title     = escapeMarkupText(element.data('title') ?? option.title ?? '');
         var use_notif = element.data('use-notification') ?? option.use_notification ?? 1;
         var alt_email = element.data('alternative-email') ?? option.alternative_email ?? '';

         var icon = "";
         var fk   = "";
         switch (itemtype) {
            case "User":
               if (items_id == 0) {
                  text = alt_email;
                  icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-mail mx-1" title="E-mail direto"></i>`;
               } else {
                  icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-user mx-1" title="Usuário"></i>`;
               }
               if ("requester" == "assign") {
                  fk = "users_id_assign";
               } else if ("requester" == "requester") {
                  fk = "users_id_requester";
               } else if ("requester" == "observer") {
                  fk = "users_id_observer";
               }
               break;
            case "Group":
               icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-users mx-1" title="Grupo"></i>`;
               if ("requester" == "assign") {
                  fk = "groups_id_assign";
               } else if ("requester" == "requester") {
                  fk = "groups_id_requester";
               } else if ("requester" == "observer") {
                  fk = "groups_id_observer";
               }
               break;
            case "Supplier":
               icon = `<i class="ti fa-fw ti-package mx-1" title="Fornecedor"></i>`;
               fk   = "suppliers_id_assign";
               break;
         }

         var actions = "";
         
         // manage specific display for tree data (like groups)
         var indent = "";
         if (!is_selection && "level" in option && option.level > 1) {
            for (let index = 1; index < option.level; index++) {
               indent = "&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"+indent;
            }
            indent = indent+"&raquo;";
         }

         // prepare html for option element
         var text = (is_selection && itemtype == "Group") ? title : text;
         var option_text    = `<span class="actor_text">${text}</span>`;
         var option_element = $(`<span class="actor_entry" data-itemtype="${itemtype}" data-items-id="${items_id}" data-actortype="${actorytype}">${indent}${icon}${option_text}${actions}</span>`);

          if (is_selection && itemtype == "User") {
              const unique_id = "user_opt_" + actor_select.attr('data-actor-type') + "User" + items_id;
              $.ajax({
                  url: '/glpi/ajax/comments.php',
                  type: 'POST',
                  data: {
                      'itemtype': 'User',
                      'value': items_id,
                  }
              }).then((result) => {
                  if (result) {
                      actor_select.parent().append('<' + `div id="content${unique_id}" style="display: none;">` + result + '<' + '/div>');
                      option_element.attr('data-glpi-popover-source', `content${unique_id}`);
                  }
              });
          }

         // manage ticket information (number of assigned ticket for an actor)
         if (is_selection && itemtype != "Email") {
            var label = '';
            if ("requester" == "assign") {
               label = "Número de chamados atribuídos";
            } else if ("requester" == "requester") {
               label = "Número de chamados como requerente";
            }
            var existing_element = $(
               `<span class="assign_infos ms-1" title="${label}"
                     data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-placement="top"
                     data-id="${items_id}" data-fk="${fk}">
                  <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>
               </span>`
            );
            option_element.append(existing_element);

            $.get("/glpi/ajax/actorinformation.php", {
               [fk]: items_id,
               only_number: true,
            }).done(function (number) {
               var badge = "";
               if (number.length > 0) {
                  badge = `<span class="badge bg-secondary-lt">
                  ${number}
               </span>`;
               }
               existing_element.html(badge);
            });
         }

         return option_element;
      };

      var select2_width = "calc(100% - 30px)";

      const actor_select = $("#actor_147568279");
      actor_select.select2({
         tags: true,
         width: select2_width,
         tokenSeparators: [',', ' '],
         disabled: false, // TODO can edit

         templateSelection: function(option) { return genericTemplate_147568279(option, true); },
         templateResult:    function(option) { return genericTemplate_147568279(option, false); },
         disabled: true,
         createTag: function (params) {
            var term = $.trim(params.term);

            if (term === '') {
               return null;
            }

            // Don't offset to create a tag if it's not an email
            if (!new RegExp(/^[\w-\.]+@([\w-]+\.)+[\w-]{2,63}$/).test(term)) {
               // Return null to disable tag creation
               return null;
            }

            return {
               id: term,
               text: term,
               itemtype: "User",
               items_id: 0,
               use_notification: 1,
               alternative_email: term,
            }
         },
         ajax: {
            url: '/glpi/ajax/actors.php',

               var is_new_item = false;

           content: function() {
               // Close other popovers
               $('.popover').popover('hide');
               return $('#' + $(this).attr('data-glpi-popover-source')).html();
           }
       }).on('hide.bs.popover', function () {
            // prevent closing popover when user card is hover
            if ($('.user-info-card:hover').length > 0) {
                return false;
            }
        });

        // when the mouse leave the user card in the popover, close it
        $(document).on('mouseleave', '.user-info-card', function() {
            setTimeout(() => {

      // manage actors change
      var updateActors147568279 = function() {
         var data = $("#actor_147568279").select2('data');

         var new_actors = [];
         data.forEach(function(selection) {
            var element = $(selection.element);

            var itemtype  = selection.itemtype ?? element.data('itemtype');
            var items_id  = selection.items_id ?? element.data('items-id');
            var use_notif = selection.use_notification  ?? element.data('use-notification')  ?? false;
            var alt_email = selection.alternative_email ?? element.data('alternative-email') ?? '';

            if (itemtype == "Email") {
               itemtype  = "User";
               use_notif = true;
               alt_email = selection.id;
            }

            new_actors.push({
               itemtype: itemtype,
               items_id: items_id,
               use_notification: use_notif,
               alternative_email: alt_email,
            });
         });

         actors[actorytype] = new_actors;

         saveActorsToDom();
      };
      $("#actor_147568279").on('select2:select', function () {
         updateActors147568279();
         
      });
      $("#actor_147568279").on('select2:unselect', function () {
         updateActors147568279();
         
      });

      // intercept event for edit notification button
      document.addEventListener('click', event => {
         if (event.target.closest("#actor_147568279 + .select2 .edit-notify-user")) {
            return openNotifyModal(event);
         }
         // if a click on assign info is detected prevent opening of select2
         if (event.target.closest("#actor_147568279 + .select2 .assign_infos")) {
            event.stopPropagation();
         }
      }, {capture: true})
      document.addEventListener('keydown', event => {
         if (event.target.closest("#actor_147568279 + .select2 .edit-notify-user")
            && event.key == "Enter") {
            return openNotifyModal(event);
         }
      }, {capture: true})

   $(function() {
      var actorytype = 'observer';

      // function to display an option in the list or the selected input
      var genericTemplate_1985336691 = function(option = {}, is_selection = false) {
         var element   = $(option.element);
         var itemtype  = element.data('itemtype') ?? option.itemtype;
         var items_id  = element.data('items-id') ?? option.items_id;
         var text      = escapeMarkupText(element.data('text') ?? option.text ?? '');
         var title     = escapeMarkupText(element.data('title') ?? option.title ?? '');
         var use_notif = element.data('use-notification') ?? option.use_notification ?? 1;
         var alt_email = element.data('alternative-email') ?? option.alternative_email ?? '';

         var icon = "";
         var fk   = "";
         switch (itemtype) {
            case "User":
               if (items_id == 0) {
                  text = alt_email;
                  icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-mail mx-1" title="E-mail direto"></i>`;
               } else {
                  icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-user mx-1" title="Usuário"></i>`;
               }
               if ("observer" == "assign") {
                  fk = "users_id_assign";
               } else if ("observer" == "requester") {
                  fk = "users_id_requester";
               } else if ("observer" == "observer") {
                  fk = "users_id_observer";
               }
               break;
            case "Group":
               icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-users mx-1" title="Grupo"></i>`;
               if ("observer" == "assign") {
                  fk = "groups_id_assign";
               } else if ("observer" == "requester") {
                  fk = "groups_id_requester";
               } else if ("observer" == "observer") {
                  fk = "groups_id_observer";
               }
               break;
            case "Supplier":
               icon = `<i class="ti fa-fw ti-package mx-1" title="Fornecedor"></i>`;
               fk   = "suppliers_id_assign";
               break;
         }

         var actions = "";
         
         // manage specific display for tree data (like groups)
         var indent = "";
         if (!is_selection && "level" in option && option.level > 1) {
            for (let index = 1; index < option.level; index++) {
               indent = "&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"+indent;
            }
            indent = indent+"&raquo;";
         }

         // prepare html for option element
         var text = (is_selection && itemtype == "Group") ? title : text;
         var option_text    = `<span class="actor_text">${text}</span>`;
         var option_element = $(`<span class="actor_entry" data-itemtype="${itemtype}" data-items-id="${items_id}" data-actortype="${actorytype}">${indent}${icon}${option_text}${actions}</span>`);

          if (is_selection && itemtype == "User") {
              const unique_id = "user_opt_" + actor_select.attr('data-actor-type') + "User" + items_id;
              $.ajax({
                  url: '/glpi/ajax/comments.php',
                  type: 'POST',
                  data: {
                      'itemtype': 'User',
                      'value': items_id,
                  }
              }).then((result) => {
                  if (result) {
                      actor_select.parent().append('<' + `div id="content${unique_id}" style="display: none;">` + result + '<' + '/div>');
                      option_element.attr('data-glpi-popover-source', `content${unique_id}`);
                  }
              });
          }

         // manage ticket information (number of assigned ticket for an actor)
         if (is_selection && itemtype != "Email") {
            var label = '';
            if ("observer" == "assign") {
               label = "Número de chamados atribuídos";
            } else if ("observer" == "requester") {
               label = "Número de chamados como requerente";
            }
            var existing_element = $(
               `<span class="assign_infos ms-1" title="${label}"
                     data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-placement="top"
                     data-id="${items_id}" data-fk="${fk}">
                  <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>
               </span>`
            );
            option_element.append(existing_element);

            $.get("/glpi/ajax/actorinformation.php", {
               [fk]: items_id,
               only_number: true,
            }).done(function (number) {
               var badge = "";
               if (number.length > 0) {
                  badge = `<span class="badge bg-secondary-lt">
                  ${number}
               </span>`;
               }
               existing_element.html(badge);
            });
         }

         return option_element;
      };

   <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function() {
      var actorytype = 'assign';

      // function to display an option in the list or the selected input
      var genericTemplate_1208725378 = function(option = {}, is_selection = false) {
         var element   = $(option.element);
         var itemtype  = element.data('itemtype') ?? option.itemtype;
         var items_id  = element.data('items-id') ?? option.items_id;
         var text      = escapeMarkupText(element.data('text') ?? option.text ?? '');
         var title     = escapeMarkupText(element.data('title') ?? option.title ?? '');
         var use_notif = element.data('use-notification') ?? option.use_notification ?? 1;
         var alt_email = element.data('alternative-email') ?? option.alternative_email ?? '';

         var icon = "";
         var fk   = "";
         switch (itemtype) {
            case "User":
               if (items_id == 0) {
                  text = alt_email;
                  icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-mail mx-1" title="E-mail direto"></i>`;
               } else {
                  icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-user mx-1" title="Usuário"></i>`;
               }
               if ("assign" == "assign") {
                  fk = "users_id_assign";
               } else if ("assign" == "requester") {
                  fk = "users_id_requester";
               } else if ("assign" == "observer") {
                  fk = "users_id_observer";
               }
               break;
            case "Group":
               icon = `<i class="ti  fa-fw ti-users mx-1" title="Grupo"></i>`;
               if ("assign" == "assign") {
                  fk = "groups_id_assign";
               } else if ("assign" == "requester") {
                  fk = "groups_id_requester";
               } else if ("assign" == "observer") {
                  fk = "groups_id_observer";
               }
               break;
            case "Supplier":
               icon = `<i class="ti fa-fw ti-package mx-1" title="Fornecedor"></i>`;
               fk   = "suppliers_id_assign";
               break;
         }

         var actions = "";
         
         // manage specific display for tree data (like groups)
         var indent = "";
         if (!is_selection && "level" in option && option.level > 1) {
            for (let index = 1; index < option.level; index++) {
               indent = "&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"+indent;
            }
            indent = indent+"&raquo;";
         }

         // prepare html for option element
         var text = (is_selection && itemtype == "Group") ? title : text;
         var option_text    = `<span class="actor_text">${text}</span>`;
         var option_element = $(`<span class="actor_entry" data-itemtype="${itemtype}" data-items-id="${items_id}" data-actortype="${actorytype}">${indent}${icon}${option_text}${actions}</span>`);

          if (is_selection && itemtype == "User") {
              const unique_id = "user_opt_" + actor_select.attr('data-actor-type') + "User" + items_id;
              $.ajax({
                  url: '/glpi/ajax/comments.php',
                  type: 'POST',
                  data: {
                      'itemtype': 'User',
                      'value': items_id,
                  }
              }).then((result) => {
                  if (result) {
                      actor_select.parent().append('<' + `div id="content${unique_id}" style="display: none;">` + result + '<' + '/div>');
                      option_element.attr('data-glpi-popover-source', `content${unique_id}`);
                  }
              });
          }

         // manage ticket information (number of assigned ticket for an actor)
         if (is_selection && itemtype != "Email") {
            var label = '';
            if ("assign" == "assign") {
               label = "Número de chamados atribuídos";
            } else if ("assign" == "requester") {
               label = "Número de chamados como requerente";
            }
            var existing_element = $(
               `<span class="assign_infos ms-1" title="${label}"
                     data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-placement="top"
                     data-id="${items_id}" data-fk="${fk}">
                  <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>
               </span>`
            );
            option_element.append(existing_element);

            $.get("/glpi/ajax/actorinformation.php", {
               [fk]: items_id,
               only_number: true,
            }).done(function (number) {
               var badge = "";
               if (number.length > 0) {
                  badge = `<span class="badge bg-secondary-lt">
                  ${number}
               </span>`;
               }
               existing_element.html(badge);
            });
         }

         return option_element;
      };

      var select2_width = "calc(100% - 30px)";

      const actor_select = $("#actor_1208725378");
      actor_select.select2({
         tags: true,

         createTag: function (params) {
            var term = $.trim(params.term);

            if (term === '') {

            }

            // Don't offset to create a tag if it's not an email

               return null;

      // manage actors change
      var updateActors1208725378 = function() {
         var data = $("#actor_1208725378").select2('data');

         var new_actors = [];
         data.forEach(function(selection) {
            var element = $(selection.element);

            var itemtype  = selection.itemtype ?? element.data('itemtype');
            var items_id  = selection.items_id ?? element.data('items-id');
            var use_notif = selection.use_notification  ?? element.data('use-notification')  ?? false;
            var alt_email = selection.alternative_email ?? element.data('alternative-email') ?? '';

            if (itemtype == "Email") {
               itemtype  = "User";
               use_notif = true;
               alt_email = selection.id;
            }

            new_actors.push({
               itemtype: itemtype,
               items_id: items_id,
               use_notification: use_notif,
               alternative_email: alt_email,
            });
         });

         actors[actorytype] = new_actors;

         saveActorsToDom();
      };
      $("#actor_1208725378").on('select2:select', function () {
         updateActors1208725378();
         
      });
      $("#actor_1208725378").on('select2:unselect', function () {
         updateActors1208725378();
         
      });

      // intercept event for edit notification button
      document.addEventListener('click', event => {
         if (event.target.closest("#actor_1208725378 + .select2 .edit-notify-user")) {
            return openNotifyModal(event);
         }
         // if a click on assign info is detected prevent opening of select2
         if (event.target.closest("#actor_1208725378 + .select2 .assign_infos")) {
            event.stopPropagation();
         }
      }, {capture: true})
      document.addEventListener('keydown', event => {
         if (event.target.closest("#actor_1208725378 + .select2 .edit-notify-user")
            && event.key == "Enter") {
            return openNotifyModal(event);
         }
      }, {capture: true})

<script type="text/javascript">
   /* global bootstrap */
   var editActorNotifySettings_modal = null;
   $(function () {
      editActorNotifySettings_modal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('editActorNotifySettings'), {});
   });

   var actors = {
               requester: [
                        {
               itemtype: "User",
               items_id: "821",
               use_notification: 1,
                                 alternative_email: "",
                           },
                        {
               itemtype: "Group",
               items_id: "109",
               use_notification: 0,
                           },
                     ],
               observer: [
                        {
               itemtype: "Group",
               items_id: "109",
               use_notification: 0,
                           },
                     ],
               assign: [
                        {
               itemtype: "User",
               items_id: "898",
               use_notification: 1,
                                 alternative_email: "",
                           },
                        {
               itemtype: "Group",
               items_id: "86",
               use_notification: 0,
                           },
                     ],
         };

   // edit email preference when .edit-notify-user button is activated
   function openNotifyModal(event) {
      event.stopPropagation();

      var element = $(event.target).closest('.actor_entry');
      var itemtype  = element.data('itemtype');
      var items_id  = element.data('items-id');
      var actortype = element.data('actortype');
      var text      = element.data('text');

      var actorIndex = actors[actortype].findIndex(element => (element.itemtype == itemtype && element.items_id == items_id));
      var actor      = actors[actortype][actorIndex];

      var modal = $('#editActorNotifySettings');
      modal.find("input[name=_notifications_actortype]").val(actortype);
      modal.find("input[name=_notifications_actorindex]").val(actorIndex);
      modal.find("input[name=_notifications_actorname]").removeAttr('readonly').val(text).attr('readonly', 'true');
      modal.find("input[name=_notifications_use_notification]").prop('checked', parseInt(actor.use_notification));
      modal.find("input[name=_notifications_alternative_email]").val(actor.alternative_email);

      editActorNotifySettings_modal.show();
   }

   // save edited actor when clicking on save button
   $(document).on('click', '#saveActorNotifySettings', function(event) {
      saveNotificationSettings();
   });

   // prevent submit on enter key in modal (but save notification settings)
   $(document).on('keyup keypress', '#editActorNotifySettings input', function(event) {
      var keyCode = event.keyCode || event.which;
      if (keyCode === 13) {
         event.preventDefault();
         saveNotificationSettings();
         return false;
      }
   });

   // save settings from modal (get modal data, and serialize them into input hidden)
   function saveNotificationSettings() {
      var modal = $('#editActorNotifySettings');
      var actortype  = modal.find("input[name=_notifications_actortype]").val();
      var actorIndex = modal.find("input[name=_notifications_actorindex]").val();
      var use_notif  = (modal.find("input[name=_notifications_use_notification]").is(":checked") ? 1 : 0);
      var alt_email  = modal.find("input[name=_notifications_alternative_email]").val();

      var actor = actors[actortype][actorIndex];
      actor.use_notification = use_notif;
      actor.alternative_email = alt_email;

      // update notif setting icon for actor
      var fa_class = "far";
      if (use_notif) {
         fa_class = "fas";
      }

      var actor_entry = $('.actor_entry[data-itemtype='+actor.itemtype+'][data-items-id='+actor.items_id+'][data-actortype='+actortype+']');

      // toggle notify icon
      actor_entry.find('.notify-icon')
         .removeClass('fas far')
         .addClass(fa_class);

      // toggle text for direct email
      if (actor.itemtype == "User" && parseInt(actor.items_id) == 0) {
         actor_entry.find('.actor_text').html(alt_email);
      }


      editActorNotifySettings_modal.hide();
      saveActorsToDom();
   }

   // save actors object to dom
   function saveActorsToDom() {
      $('#_actors').val(JSON.stringify(actors));
   }
   saveActorsToDom();
</script>

      </div>
